<Author>AllyPallyBristol
<Content>Excellent breakfast staff In addition to all the other comments made about this hotel, I feel that I would like to thank the breakfast lady for her excellent service. Our daughter who has a nut allergy wanted to eat one of the freshly baked croissants that were on the breakfast table. I checked first with the lady who was serving at breakfast and she didn't know if they contained nuts or not because they were supplied by a local bakery. She got straight on the phone to the bakery and spoke to the baker himself who was able to give her a list of all the ingredients. In this day and age of mass-produced food we were so impressed with being able to speak directly to the person who had baked the pastries. There is no way that you could do that in England--everything these days seems to come from some huge bakehouse and transported miles by road. I am sorry that I didn't get her name but that was first-class customer service. By the way, the hotel provides a splendid continental breakfast, with a wide choice of freshly produced breads, pastries, cakes and accompanying yoghurts, ham, cheese, cerial and fruit. Plus you can ask for a genuine Italian latte which comes in a glass!!

<Author>maryefinucan
<Content>Excellent Service and Great Location Stayed at this hotel pre/post on a cruise out of Venice. The locationis great -- close to the bus terminal for transportation to/from the airport and cruise terminal. (Only needed to carry our luggage acrosstwo bridges.) It's a bit of a walk to the major attractions, but veryclose to the vaparetto stop. On the other hand, the neighborhood isn't nearly as crazy crowded as those nearer to San Marco.The staff couldn't have been nicer. Very friendly and helpful, excellent English. Gave us recommendations for restaurants in the area and good advice on how to get around.The rooms are fairly small, typical of Europe. Three of us were givena small suite in a beautifully renovated annex just down the calle from the main building. It had a bedroom and separate living room with a sofa bed. Perfect for us. (Not a lot of room for luggage, however.)The only problem was the shower in the bathroom which had no bracket for hanging the hose. Rather awkward. The staff assured us this will be fixed soon -- now that the August everything closes down in Italy season is over.All in all, we all enjoyed this hotel very much and highly recommend it.

<Author>Juantwo
<Content>Wonderful Staff We stayed at this wonderful little hotel for 2 nights in early September. The staff is just great and the location is very good. The rooms are quite spacious and the bathrooms in particular are well appointed.  The staff will go out of there way to make reservations for restaurants and any other services you may need. If at all possible go to the Osterio al Vecio Pozzo restaurant which is tucked into a side street behind the hotel. Absolutely fabulous and a great value. The hotel people recommended it to us! A word of caution to Venezia travelers. The train station is across the Canal from the hotel. However it is very difficult to get your baggage over the bridge especially if it is heavy.We hired a porter and paid him $8 euro per bag and it was well worth it. <Author>Leeds7
<Content>Way above average service I just can't say enough about the level of service at this hotel - I've travelled extensively to some very expensive hotels and this is the best service I've encountered anywhere. They upgraded me free of charge to a beautiful canal view room which was tasteful a good size and spotless. If you're worried about noise, don't go for the canal view (could be why I got the room I guess being on the younger side of the guests staying there) - the noise on the street served as a great alarm clock in the morning. The location is great - not for charm but convenience - directly opposite the train station and very close to the bus station, also directly opposite the vaporetto, so perfect really. the ground floor which includes the breakfast area is tiny, really small and not as tastefully decorated as the rooms but it's fine. You can eat outside by the canal although it's pretty busy with people arriving with suitcases etc. although really not a problem either. The food is as good as any other hotel in Italy I've experienced, they could probably do more if they had more space. In short the crowning glory of this hotel is its staff from chamber maids, to waitress to manager, they are all genuine, cheerful but not overbearing - and the manager (I think he was the manager) could not have gone out of his way more for me or anyone else I saw him dealing with. As a woman travelling on her own I felt very safe and comfortable here.

<Author>swatts1
<Content>Excellent hotel!!!! I booked this hotel months before our trip based on excellent reviews from this site. I was not disappointed in any way. This was our 2nd visit to Venice and Hotel Antiche Figure provided the perfect location for our stay. I contacted the hotel directly to make reservations. We needed a triple for two nights prior to our cruise and one additional night after the cruise. Normally they don't book one night on a Saturday night, but kindly made an exception since we were booked to stay several nights before the cruise. All dealings with them were timely, positive, and friendly. Several days before we were due to arrive a possible train strike in Germany meant that we needed to get to Venice a day early. An email to the hotel easily arranged an additional night. The location was very convenient to the train station, though we had to lug our heavy suitcases over a very steep bridge. We arrived late at night when restaurants were closed, but the management got some food and wine rustled up so that we didn't go to bed hungry. The room was absolutely beautiful, overlooking the Grand Canal. It was huge and the bathroom was also very large and very modern. The management of the hotel was accommodating in many ways. They suggested Osterias and Trattorias. They also arranged a water taxi to take us to the cruise ship as well as to the airport when we left Venice. I give this hotel and its management my highest praise and will stay there again any time I return to Venice.

<Author>Fwapsk
<Content>2 nights - nice and convenient! We stayed here for two nights in August and it was our first trip to Venice. Very nice hotel, convenient location right next to Piazza Roma (where you arrive when you take a bus from Marco Polo Airport). Hotel staff was very pleasant and helpful, bartender was interested in America, etc. The convenience is huge for first time visitors to Venice, because fighting the mobs through the narrow streets and on the Vaporetto may be intimidating and stressful with lots of luggage to get to another hotel. Vaporetto stops right across the canal for easy access throughout Venice, or you can walk through the meandering streets for a great experience. Venice is beautiful, but it is a 100% tourist destination so expect lots of people. Got to the island of Burano - its beautiful! Torcello is very quiet and remote and probably ok to miss.

<Author>Faience44
<Content>Excellent base from which to explore Venice Based on the glowing user reviews at tripadvisor.com I decided early on that I wanted to stay here with my famiy when we visited Venice. I booked in early February after a long conversation during which I made clear that I wanted two joined rooms for our family of three. This turned out not to be possible (the hotel was planning to introduce apartments in a separate building, but they weren't in service at that point, I was told) so I settled for a three-person room overlooking the canal.The one big advantage of the Antiche Figure is that you can get there by foot in about three minutes from the station, saving you the need to fight your way onto a vaporetto with bags. The first impression of the room was not good, since we were bowled over by the smell of cigarette smoke when we opened the door. I went down to reception and was told they had no record of a specific request for a non-smoking room (although they knew we were travelling with a young child).Overall, we enjoyed our stay. The breakfasts were very good.The room was air conditioned, comfortable and not too noisy despite facing on to the canal, although you won't be able to sleep in much beyond 7.30 am when the boat traffic really starts up. There are plenty of vaporetto stops outside the station which makes exploring the city very easy. There also is a high-speed internet terminal in reception for clients, which I found useful.The one thing that did bug me was that every time I was in reception and guests came in, I seemed to hear them being told their apartments were ready or that they were being upgraded to a suite at no extra charge. The hotel had known in early February that I really wanted an apartment or suite-type arrangement andyet they made no effort to inform me when these types of accommodations became available. I'd willingly have paid the extra.  
<Date>Aug 23, 2007

<Author>JohnnyJetLag
<Content>Fantastic, Friendly Hotel Just got back from a night stay in this excellent hotel. We've stayed there three times on three seperate occasions, and will deffinately stay here again the next time we're back in Venice. It's location is great for ease of access to the Bus Terminal, Train Station (directly opposite) and the majority of the major Vaporetto routes. There's a Gondola pick up point right outside too, which if you ask at the reception desk they can get you a discount. If you plan to visit Murano to see the glass blowing factories, It's also worth asking at reception as they can get you a free taxi ride to one of the factories on the island with no obligation to purchase anything.Of the three rooms that we've had, they've all been fantastic. Spacious by european standards, fully air conditioned and with a well appointed bathroom. Breakfast isn't included (I believe) in the normal price, but they do a deal with those that have booked through expedia (and maybe other online agencies) of a continental style buffet breakfast for éˆ§?. I think that's great value, as you'd be hard pressed to find this price anywhere else.The bar area is great, and they do have chairs and tables outside so that you can watch people passing and boats chugging up and down the grand canal. The adjacent reception area also has a free internet access point. Above all, this is a friendly and relaxing hotel that we will always come back to.

<Author>aphrodite100
<Content>Fantastic hotel We spent three nights at the hotel as part of our Grand Tour of Europe honeymoonOn arrival, we were given the choice of a room in the hotel, or, for the same price, a larger room in the annexe at the back. We were the first people to stay on the second floor and gave the room a test drive. Room was charming, with canopied four-poster bed, huge shower with massage jets, and bath robes and slippers. Obviously no view of the Grand Canal, and no lift (unlike the main building) but extremely comfortableWe found the 5 Euro breakfast excellent value - and took the advice of Tripadvisors to have non-machine made cappucinos. Cereal, fruit, croissants, eggs, cold meats, pastries, fruit juice - and we finished our breakfast by taking our last cappucino and a slice of fruit pie outside to watch the world go by on the Grand Canal (worth 5 Euros alone!) I have no idea where people would go to get a better value breakfast in VeniceThe hotel is a vaporetto ride from St Mark's Square, but we found this to be beneficial as the squares and canals behind the hotel were much less crowded and interesting to explore. Great location for the train station or the Piazza Roma where we left our car (just two bridges to negotiate)Staff were excellent and informative, and sitting at one of the tables in the evening drinking Prosecco or Peach Bellinis just people watching is one of the highlights of our honeymoonAbsolutely intend to return, but with less baggage!

<Author>Angelzoey2
<Content>Great location We stayed at Hotel Antiche Figure for three nights during our honeymoon and found it to be the perfect hotel for a stay in one of the most romantic cities in the world. While the hotel is located on the opposite end of all the attractions (St. Mark's Square, Doge's Palace, etc.), it was nice to be near the quieter part of the city, but yet still be on the Grand Canal. Plus, Venice is so small we had fun just walking to places like St. Mark's, being that it would only take about 20-25 minutes to walk there (And who doesn't love walking through Venetian cobblestone streets!)The hotel was a 5 minute walk to both the ATV (water bus) and to Piazzale Roma, which is where we had to pick up the shuttle to the cruise we were taking from Venice. To get to the airport you can either, very easily, take the ATV to the airport or pick up an actual taxi (driven) from Piazzale Roma, which is connected by bridge to the mainland. Another benefit was the hotel was right next to one of the only three bridges that crosses the Grand Canal, so we didn't have to walk far to get to the other side. The only downside to the hotel was the 5 euro breakfast. It served cold lunchmeat, cereal and fruit, not enough to fill our bellies before walking around for 10 hours. I would suggest saving your money for a slice of Italian pizza.

<Author>LITSBostonMA
<Content>Loved Antiche Figure!! We have just returned from 4 nights at Hotel Anitche Figure in Venice. We stayed there prior to boarding the Splendour of the Sea on a Greek Island cruise. The hotel is on the grand canal and beautifully maintained. The service is fantastic and all of the staff we met were charming and friendly. The hotel is right across from the train station and next to the major port and bus stop - we were able to walk with our luggages to get on the cruiseship. The four of us stayed in 2 separate rooms, I believe rooms can only accommodate a maximum of 3 people. My two daughters had their own room close by and the rooms are very comfortable with beautiful bathrooms. The included breakfast is simple but really tasty with enough items to keep us going for the whole day. We hiked/walked to the famous San Marco Square every day. It was an advanture to take a different route on a daily basis. We enjoyed sitting in front of the hotel in the late afternoon with wine and snack looking at all the passerbys. It was a positive that the hotel is not at the center of the tourist area around San Marco. The shops around tend to have better prices and are less crowded than around San Marco and the Rialto Bridge. The staff also showed us some new residential units, i.e., apartments that are part of the hotel in the street next to the hotel. Since it was our first time in Venice, we wanted to be overlooking the grand canal, but we will definitely consider staying at those units the next time. We will definitely go back to Hotel Anitche Figure when we plan on returning to Venice.

The hotel staff were very friendly and went out of their way to help in any way they could. Check in was quick and easy. Our hotel room overlooked the Canal and was clean, spacious and quiet. The hotel stored our luggage for us on check out day while we explored Venice until our 2:30 train departure. I would highly recommend this hotel if you are staying in Venice.

<Author>RonaldoC
<Content>Fantastic Little hotel I am currently on a two night stay at the Hotel Antiche Figure, Venezia as the final leg of my trip to Italy. A lot has already been said about this hotel, the quality of the rooms, the friendly staff etc and they are all true so I wonéˆ¥æª› go into too much detail. What I will say is that I thought the location was really good. If you are arriving by train then it really is only across the Ponte dei Scalzi, just a couple of minutes walk. Ok the bridge is very steep and it can get very hot in Venice at this time of year but if you are incapable of taking your luggage over this bridge then I would suggest that Venice is probably not the best place for you to visit as it does involve a great deal of walking and climbing over bridges (after all there are over 1000 of them). OK there are probably more central locations down the Grand Canal but these are generally more expensive and I would suggest not such good value for money as the Antiche Figure.I booked the hotel entirely on the strength of the TA reviews giving this hotel a #3 status in Venice went a long way and as usual TA visitors did not let me down. The hotel management obviously keep an eye on this website as they posted a retort to one review a couple of days ago which is one of the great things about this site and is what makes it unbiased. Anyway if they are reading this after I post it just send the Champagne to the room ;-).I booked through an agent (otel.com) but then on the off chance e-mailed the hotel directly to see if they had a canal view room. They replied promptly and for 40 euros per night extra I was upgraded to room 212 which had a small balcony, one of only two with a balcony overlooking the canal. This was a great little bonus as I really enjoyed sitting there watching the hustle and bustle of the canal especially waking up at 06:30 and watching the local papers being delivered along with everything else Venice needs during the day. As previous reviews have said the ACTV stop Ferrovia is directly across from the hotel so you only have to cross the ponte and you can go wherever you like in Venice by vaparetto. One way trips cost 6 euros and 24 hour tickets 15 euros (no reduction for children). You can also get 12, 48  72 hour tickets, see the ACTV website. Remember to validate your ticket in the yellow stamping machines, I nearly got into trouble for this. If in doubt the staff in the hotel will give you more info. Use the #1 or #82 line to get all the way down the Grand Canal and to the Piazza San Marco. The 82 is a little quicker as it has fewer stops. Alternatively you can order a water taxi to get you wherever you want to go.Anyway I was gonna keep this one short so in summary this is a nice, comfortable, well run hotel. The location is great for getting in and out of Venice especially if you are arriving for the first time and anyway Venice is a small city so itéˆ¥æªš not really an issue unless you really want to stay nearer the so called hotspots. The rooms are well appointed and clean. Staff are great. The internet connection is FREE just ask for a LAN cable at the front desk (my campaign for hotels to provide free internet access is gaining support at last) which is fantastic since it cost me 15 euros a night in Rome. The breakfast is good, probably not the best in the world as already stated by the manager, but a good choice of pastries, drinks etc. You are not going to get a good oléˆ¥?American/English breakfast in Venice as far as I can see so when in Venezia etc. It was sufficient for me before a long walk around Venice.I would heartily recommend this hotel to anyone.

<Author>pattkark
<Content>Wonderful Hotel and Staff My husband and I stayed at the Antiche Figure for three nights in June in a Deluxe room overlooking the canal. We arrived in Venice via an overnight train from Paris and were thrilled that we had such a short walk to the hotel. Yes... the bridge is steep, but very manageable. Just rest at the top! The hotel is lovely downstairs. There is a small lobby and a bar area. The breakfast room is also on this floor and is very nice and quite adequate for all of the guests. But the best seats are outside at one of the many tables right on the canal. It was a lot of fun to sit and watch Venice go by! Our room was quite large with several windows which opened up to the canal. It was fun to sit in the window in the afternoon and watch the gondoliers get ready for the afternoon gondola rides. The room/bathroom was very clean and the bed was VERY comfortable. Our room had a King bed with sitting area and desk. We slept with the window open and could hear the water at night and in the morning. After 10pm, it was very quiet outside except for an occasional boat. I thought the room on the canal was worth the extra price.The location was great for us since we arrived and departed by train. I was also happy to retreat from the crowds and noise at San Marco's Square to our quiet hotel. Walking was not a problem in Venice since the city isn't that large. You will get lost, but that is part of the fun. Just relax. The best part of the hotel is the staff. We stayed in 6 hotels on our 3-week trip and the staff at Antiche Figure was by far the most helpful and conscience of all of the hotels we visited (and they were all nice hotels). We were spoiled by good service after leaving the Antiche Figure. The staff always made you feel as though you were the only one they were assisting. Even the young woman at breakfast was so friendly and helpful it made you look forward to breakfast each morning. Speaking of breakfast, I will have to disagree with a previous reviewer. As I said, we stayed in 5 other hotels on our trip and the breakfast at Antiche Figure was right on par with every other hotel. They offered a good variety with pasteries, meats, cheeses, eggs, cereal, yogurt, cookies, and various beverages. And we thoroughly enjoyed having our breakfast on the patio each morning and watching the city start to come to life. I would definitely stay here again and would recommend this hotel to all of my friends.  
<Date>Jul 6, 2007

<Author>kissel
<Content>Great stay at the Antiche Figure The AF did not disappoint, especially given our extremely high expectations from consistently strong reviews on TA. We were fortunate to be upgraded to a wonderfully large canal view room (with a surprisingly plush bathroom) on the top floor. We loved eating the fantastic breakfast buffet and enjoying pre-dinner cocktails outside along the grand canal. The hotel staff take their TA reputation extremely seriously, and could not be more friendly and accomodating to maintain their well deserved high grades. The AF is well located across the canal from the train station and vaporetto stop. However, while I felt the accomodations and service at the AF are excellent, I'm not sure I agree that the AF is deserving of its TA designation as Best for Romance in Europe. I would expect this distinction to imply that there is something extremely special about the property itself (e.g. well-maintained grounds, charming public areas, or spectacular views) and I wouldn't say the AF offers this, relative to other properties we've stayed at in Europe. However, the AF is a great hotel and is highly recommended for your stay in Venice.

<Author>AGTraveller
<Content>some specifics I agree that the location is a plus. But you should know that walking over the bridge to and from the train station is not the cinch that some seem to imply. The bridge that you need to cross is high and there are steps to climb up and down. Also, as Rick Steve points out in his guide book: staying in this area you are constantly jostling with a lot of people hauling their luggage to and from the train station. It's not a big detriment but still something to take into consideration.Also, this area is not known for great restaurants and as has been pointed out you need to take the vaporetto to go to the main tourist attractions. I don't mean to ding the hotel but its internet connection in the room is ethernet only. However, there is good wireless access downstairs in the lobby. The breakfast buffet is not something that I will remember with fond memory.I have not stayed in other hotels in Venice and perhaps by comparison this place is a gem, but for the money I pay I would expect a lot more elsewhere.

<Author>DaJoos
<Content>A Good Choice in Venice We returned from Venice and the Hotel Antiche Figure a week or so ago, and as we found all the excellent hotels by using TA I thought I should at a miniumum add my review - I'm glad to for this very nice hotel.I chose the Antiche Figure after browsing TA for a reasonably priced (by summer Venice standards!) hotel that sounded like a good match for myself, wife and 11 year old daughter. The high rankings of the Antiche Figure made me book a room.Venice was the last stop on our Italy vacation and by the time we arrived we were dragging a bit - the proximity to the train station (where we arrived) was a BIG plus, as was the warm welcome of the front desk staff. (It should be noted, however, that even though the hotel is a short bridge crossing from the train station, the bridge has no ramps - you'll have to 'lug' your luggage up and down stairs. No slight on the hotel, of course, but older travelers may want to know this).As stated the front desk staff was friendly and professional througout our stay - they took the time to welcome us each time we entered, and spent a long time orienting us to Venice when we first arrived.The room we received was the smallest of the four we stayed at in Italy, and looked out on an alley rather than the Grand Canal. Although I'd asked and hoped for a front-facing room I was told (or interpreted from the web site?) that if you have more than 2 persons the rooms don't face the front (don't take this as absolute - I *think* this is the case). Our alley-facing room was not a surprise, but I would have preferred and paid for a front-facing room if it had been available.It was clear that the room we got, with a 'matrimonial bed' (two twins pushed together) and another twin for our daughter, was originally designed for just the matrimonial bed. The large bed was pushed out of alignment with the headboard (attached to the wall), and one side bedstand had been turned sideways so they could stuff the extra twin in. This made the drawers on the bedstand useless (they were blocked) and the extra twin blocked what would have been the desk area. Not a great setup but we didn't let it spoil our stay (perhaps we should have complained?). As long as we coordinated our movements through the room all was OK.The hotel is far from St. Marks, but as Venice is small and I enjoy the vaporettos anyway this wasn't really a negative - could have been a plus due to the relative quiet. On the other hand the hotel is very close to the train station (as noted), a major water taxi stand, and the Roma (?) parking lot/bus stand which we used for transportation to the airport.The hotel breakfast was standard Italian and was offered both inside and out on the patio - a nice touch. My wife and I found food we liked but they could probably provide a few different items for children (pre-sweetened cereal, for instance). A free computer with Internet access is available across from the front desk - though with just 1 computer we could have had problems waiting we didn't have this happen during our brief checks of email.I would recommend this hotel to others who like its convenience, and would suggest that time is taken to clarify just what kind of room you receive in advance, so as to assuage any disappointment.  
<Date>Jun 29, 2007

<Content>Eveerything great My wife and I couldn't have been more happy with our choice of hotel in Venice. The hotel staff is very friendly and gives great advice on restaurants etc. Also, our booking didn't have breakfast, but they offered us to add the breakfast buffet anyway. <Author>chuckgnj
<Content>Beautiful location We stayed at this hotel for one night before a Greek cruise. The staff, especially Gianni were very helpful both while booking the hotel and when we arrived. We were given a beautiful ttriple room with a tiny balcony overlooking the Grand Canal. What a view to have for our first, but certainly not last, visit to Venice.The room was clean and the bathroom large and well-equipped with two sinks. The breakfast room was a bit small, but the food was good. There are also several tables outside which can provide a good spot for people watching or just sipping a cocktail from the hotel bar after a day of sightseeing.The hotel is across from the train station and just a couple of blocks from the Piazzale Roma. Very convenient for travelers. It is about 25 minutes stroll to San Marco, but there is much less traffic and the prices for accommodations and food are cheaper in the area around the hotel. Let me say that Venice is NOT a cheap place to stay, but if you order meals carefully, you can avoid breaking the bank.All in all, the stay at the Antiche Figure was very enjoyable and I would suggest it for travelers to Venice.

<Author>GrahamClarke
<Content>One of the best This hotel is one of the best I've ever stayed in! My husband took me as a 40th birthday present and we chose the hotel on the strength of trip advisor reviews and we found them to be very accurate. Its location is perfect - just opposite the railway and vaporetto stations and only a short walk from the bus station- believe me when you're carrying luggage it's a brilliant place to be! We had a side room (314) which was a bit small, but beautifully appointed with fabric walls, murano glass chandelier and the most comfortable bed I have ever slept in on holiday. The bathroom was beautiful and the towels were changed daily. I would say not having a room overlooking the canal was an advantage because the traffic on the canal can be noisy and is ceaseless - think of the M25! The staff are wonderfully friendly and helpful but not intrusive - spending time with you on arrival advising you of places to go and where to eat and will book tickets for concerts or the doges palace for you. Take advantage of this as we never got to the basilica because of the queues. Don't go to Venice expecting to be wowed by the cuisine. We found the restaurants to be plentiful, but mostly offering the same dishes and at very expensive prices. Expect to pay around 50 euros for a 2 course meal for 2 with house wine, but service charges are added usually at around 12% so there's no need to tip.Go over the Scalzi bridge outside the hotel to the Cannaregio district in the evening for a stroll. The area is lively and bright with glass shops and street artists. You can walk all the way to the Rialto bridge along a main street with wonderful shopping opportunities and views around every corner. We found the prices and variety here for glass and jewellery to be the best in Venice but don't be afraid to keep looking until you find what you really want as no two shops are quite the same.Murano is very pretty and very clean. There's an abundance of glass shops and we found the staff to be friendly and happy to let you look so don't be pressured into buying anything you don't want. The glass museum is worth a visit too for the 4m chandelier and the miniature formal garden all made out of glass.  
<Date>Jun 6, 2007

<Author>Coco#55
<Content>Loved the Antiche Figure We were 5 ladies travelling throughout Italy and Venice was our first stop, arriving from Rome via train. I had contacted the hotel and told them we might be late in the evening as we were arriving from the US and taking the train from Rome to Venice. Well, we arrived around 10:30 pm and as soon as we walked in...the hotel is directly across the canal from the train station...we were greeted as long lost relatives. Tony, at the front desk was so welcoming and our rooms...we had a double and a triple...were all set and ready for us weary travellers. The rooms were perfect, not too small and nicely appoited. The bathrooms were an excellent size and the beds were comfortable.The rates included breakfast which was in the back room on the main floor, small but accomodating with the usual fare. There are also small tables and chairs outside to have a drink and watch the world go bye and a small bar in the lobby for a good cocktail at the end of the day. I asked the hotel in advance to get us reservations for the Secret Tour at the Dodge's Palace and we had reservations for the next day at 10:30.The also recommended a nice restaurant the next evening for dinner in the neighborhood, which was excellent.They have free internet in the lobby which is a nice touch, so we could all let our families know we arrived safely. They did mention to me that they are in the process of adding more rooms, but these would be mini-apt, ideal for families. The location of the hotel is perfect if you are using the train station, very easy to get to with luggage. I have stayed in Venice several times, and at hotels within this area and I like this hotel by far the best. The other hotels treat you like paying guests, this hotel treats you like family. While it is a walk from St. Mark's , you can easily hop on a vaporetto, directly across the bridge, and in no time you are there, or you can walk..a wonderful way to see the real Venice and all the interesting shops, etc. along the way.I will definately come back to the Antiche Figure.

<Author>Heulwendeg
<Content>Worthy of all the praises ! We booked this hotel having read the reviews on Tripadvisor and it certainly lived up to all the previous praises. It is in an excellent position, near to the airport , the railway station and the vaporetti stops, facing the Grand Canal. We paid extra for a room overlooking the canal and it was well worth the extra cost -elegant furnishings, very good beds and spectacular views. The hotel is clean and very comfortable, it has a warm and welcoming atmosphere but its greatest strength is the staff. We arrived with a problem - Easyjet lost our suitcase for the duration of our stay. All the managerial staff speak excellent English and they took on the problem for us, ringing the airline everyday, sorting out our prebooked visit to the Doge's Palace (paperwork was in suitcase) and generally helping and supporting us. It was just like staying with friends and we are very grateful to them. We will certainly return there and until then, grazie Gianni, Francesca, Alessandro and all the staff at Hotel Antiche Figure.

<Author>Esther32
<Content>Great Hotel, Great location We stayed here only one night and one long day in April 2007. The location was very good for what we wanted. It was located right on the Grand Canal but quite west right across the Scalzi Bridge. It is across the canal from the train station and a 7 minute walk from Piazzelle Roma. We arrived very early in the morning having just left a cruise ship. We did not expect to be able to get our room so early and were prepared to stash our bags and run. However, the woman at the front desk had knowledge of us from our email correspondence and told us to wait in the breakfast room and that she would send the housekeeper up immediately to do our room. She gave us the hotel brochure, circled the windows of our room and in a 1/2 hour we were in the room. All this before 9:30 am. The view from our room was breathtaking. The service otherwise was very helpful and warm. We would stay here again without hesitation.It is in the San Croce area right near a vaporetto stop. The breakfast was good, free internet access with a cable they supply. Bathroom with little crystal chandeliers, toothbruses and other nice ammenities.

<Author>JuliaLancashire
<Content>Can't wait to go back to the Antiche Figure! After reading Trip Advisor's comments about this hotel I decided to book this for our 20th Wedding Anniversary. I am so glad I did!!The location is fantastic! Just 5 minutes walk away from the bus station and over the bridge to the train station and water bus, the hotel enabled us to get around Venice very easily.We upgraded to the Deluxe room which was lovely as it was a huge room, tastefully decorated (feel the fabric on the walls) and the bed was massive! Francesca and Alessandro were most helpful in recommending places to eat and the best way to get around and places to see.There was a lot of choice for breakfast. Breadrolls, meats, cheeses, eggs, fruit, yogurts, cereals, croissants and cake. Also tea, coffee, juice and milk.  We bought a 72 hour ticket for the water taxi and found we got value for money doing this. Most days we caught the number 83 watertaxi to the Rialto bridge and followed the signs Per S Marco. This took us through all the lovely streets to St Mark's Square. Spend time there and soak up the atmosphere, it was truly amazing! Go to the roof of St Mark's and see the four horses, we could have spent ages up there admiring the views. To get back to the hotel you could take a number 1 watertaxi from St Mark's Square to the Ferruvio (train station) or like us wander through the street following the signs Per Piazzale Roma. Don't worry you can't get lost and it is a good way of seeing all the little squares, churches, cafes, shops and a good excuse to rest on a bench to eat ice cream! When I booked this trip I really wasn't certain what to expect from Venice, some people said it smelled and it was old and dirty. All I can say is ignore it. Go and see for yourself. I fell in love with the city, it was SO much better that I could ever imagine. I would recommend this hotel to anyone as I would certainly go there again, in fact I can't wait until the next time I do!  
<Date>Apr 28, 2007

<Author>andycrawf
<Content>What a find This was our first trip to Venice, a special surprise birthday treat for my wife. Not many hotels have as many good reviews as the Antiche Figure and I did wonder if it might be a case of 'the emperors new clothes' but I decided to trust my fellow travellers... and I am glad I did. I was also a little concerned whether the view of the railway station might not exactly be the best in town, but I needn't have worried. The Grand Canal is something else, a liquid main street, and the hustle and bustle on the water and beside it is so engaging.Our hotel room was on the top floor at the front, overlooking the Grand Canal. It was beautifully decorated, very comfortable and, with the windows closed, completely peaceful. The bathroom was excellent. We received a lovely welcome from Francesca at reception who gave us lots of information about exploring the city. She advised us of two restaurants that are quite close to the hotel, both of which were excellent recommendations. They were booked for us by the hotel and the staff at the restaurants welcomed us and looked after us very well.I could wax lyrical about Venice - 3 days is just not enough and we will return... and to the Antiche Figure. It really is a great little hotel, with everything accessible, close enough to the city life yet away from the really touristy bits of San Marco.A couple of tips - take the bus from the airport to Piazzale Roma. The hotel is just 5 minutes walk from there. It is quick and cheap.Take a gondola ride, but book it yourself with the gondoliers outside the hotel, it is cheaper than the hotel arranging it. We did a night ride and I would thoroughly recommend doing it then, you see the city in a different light (excuse the pun).Take the free water taxi from the hotel to Murano (paid by the glass factory). The water taxi is a great ride but expensive if you have to pay it yourself. You just have to make your excuses at the factory for not buying their glass (phenomenally expensive, like thousands of Euros for a single piece) - but that was part of the fun!Use the Vaporettos - cheap, convenient and accessible from and to everywhere.

<Author>Springfield-Traveler
<Content>Warm, friendly Hotel We recently returned from our second trip to Italy, and our second stay at the Antiche Figure Hotel in Venice. The first trip, we relyed on Hotels.com to help us find a good hotel, and we were so pleased with this wonderful, little hotel.First of all, it has a fantastic location. Our first trip, we came in from Marco Polo Airport, via the bus, which dropped us off at Piazelle Roma, which is a transportation hub. We hopped a vaporetto (water bus) to find our hotel, and there it was, on the right side in full view! We got off at the first stop, Ferrovia,and walked across the bridge to the hotel. We couldn't believe that it was that convenient. It is also across the Grand Canal from the train station, which also came in handy for both of our trips to and from other cities. Remember that Venice is unlike other cities where one can hail a cab and be dropped right in front of your hotel. Their location is fantastic!As we walked trhrough the front door, we were greeted warmly by Alessandro, the hotel manager, who was very helpful in orienting us to the city of Venice, as well. During our three day stay, we were always treated like a member of the family by this warm and friendly staff. They all spoke English, too.The rooms are very pretty and comfortable. It is my understanding that the Grand Canal side rooms are larger, and that was where we stayed both visits. The bathrooms are very nice, too, with a bathtub and shower and a nice sized vanity.As I said earlier, we just returned from our second trip to Venice and a big reason for returning was the Antiche Figure. We have sent friends to stay there, as well, and I highly recommend this hotel.As a final note, I celebrated my birthday there last week and planned on a gondola ride, which Gianni, at the front desk, arranged for us. He escorted us to the gondola (again, right out in front of the hotel) and then quickly went back in to their bar and returned with an ice bucket and my favorite white wine, courtesy of the hotel! He even made me a birthday card on the hotel computer and presented it with the wine. Needless, to say, I was very touched by his thoughtfulness!  
<Date>Mar 29, 2007

<Author>Alexcat
<Content>Nice hotel My husband stayed at the hotel for 3 nights in March. I selected it based on the reviews on Trip Advisor. I enjoyed my stay at the hotel but to be honest I was expecting a little bit more from the hotel based on the over the top reviews. We booked a canal view room (Room 111). It was a fairly large room with a view of the Grand Canal. It was clean  nicely decorated. The room looked just like it shows on the website. The bed we had was 2 twin beds pushed together (very normal in Europe) however the beds were not quite an equal height. The side closest to the door way was slightly lower and a bit worn. In fact the foot of the bed had a rather big indentation. I wanted to mention this to the hotel but my husband wouldn't let me (it was his side of the bed). I was just a little disappointed considering we paid 239 euros for the first night  299 euros for each of the next two nights.I want to clarify that the hotel is nice but I didn't see why the reviews are as incredible as they are. I must give props to the staff. They were very helpful when we checked in - providing us with information about the vaperatos and also when we needed a water taxi for our very early flights home. I am in no way bad mouthing this hotel as it is a nice 3 star hotel. The location is perfect for those who have lots of luggage  don't want to haul them on a vaperato or pay for a water taxi.

<Author>Cassiu5
<Content>Excellent value in an expensive city I stayed at the Hotel Antiche Figure at the end of February / beginning of March. The hotel is located opposite the train station, and about 5 minutes walk from the bus station. However, if you arrive by airport shuttle late at night be prepared to get lost between the bus station and the hotel.The hotel rooms are very clean and spacious, the beds are comfortable, and the bathrooms sparkling and well equipped with both bath and shower (but make sure you learn your 'C's and 'F's if you don't want a shock). The bedroom is equipped with an in room safe, basic TV stations (CNN and BBC World for English speakers) and chandalier lighting. You can pay extra for a view of the Grande Canal, however, my view of the building opposite let me know whether it was raining or not in the morning, which was important.While the hotel is 20 minutes or so from St Marks Square this does mean you have ample opportunity to explore the side alleys on the way and discover those quiet hidden 'village squares' with kids playing and locals chatting in cafes. Getting lost is a real treat in Venice, even at night. Also, being on the Grande Canal opposite the Ferrovia boat stop means there are no fewer than nine different boat routes that will take you back to the hotel (in fact every boat on the Grande Hotel stops opposite the hotel). This means you can enjoy the boat trip from St Marks Square to the hotel late at night, when Venice seems so much more peaceful. You wouldn't do this if you stayed in an expensive hotel near St Marks. You can also catch a boat direct to Murano from opposite the hotel.The hotel staff are very helpful, and can book almost any ticket for evening concerts (at no extra charge) as well as recommend excellent restaurants (usually those recommended by other visitors). The breakfast may be extra, depending on who you book with, but the buffet of rolls, orange juice, ham, cheese, yoghurts, croissants and various pastries provide an excellent start to the day (plus tea in a pot!). The foyer also has a laptop with internet access free of charge to residents.I would defintely stay here again on my next trip to VeniceFinally, don't worry, the lift floor always makes that noise when you get in.  
<Date>Mar 5, 2007

<Content>Rip Off My wife and I stayed in Hotel Antiche Figure from 7th to 11th Feb.First impressions were that it was just adequate. It was easy to get to from piazza roma where bus depot is. My room was éˆ§?39(éˆ§?0 extra for canal view) a night plus basic breakfast. The hotel will probably dissagree but in my opinion it was basic. Now I have been in a lot of cities around europe and most hotels I have stayed in are of a much better quality for a more reasonable price. We were disgusted with the restaurant recommendation by the hotel.Now this hotel is not I repeat not near St.Marks Square.Between walking to, waiting, travelling on water bus it takes about 45 mins. <Author>Haymusos
<Content>The perfect Venetian place to stay I can't recommend this fantastic little hotel enough. This was our second stay here, our first in the summer last year and most recently at the beginning of February with our parents. Both experiences were of the highest standard - where do I start?The hotel was so simple to find and incredibly convenient. It's directly opposite the train station (a very nice train station - not unsightly at all!) and just 5 minutes walk and a couple of small bridges away from the Piazzale Roma (the main bus station, connecting you to the mainland and airport). Right from the moment we arrived (we were early both times) we were greeted by Gianni who was very friendly and couldn't help us enough. We were shown immediately to our rooms. We paid extra for the canal view which I believe was definitely worth it. Room 412 on the top floor was particularly lovely. The rooms are clean and beautifully furnished in typical Venetian decor. Comfy beds, gorgeous bathroom, mini-bar, tv, hairdryer etc. Cleaned every day including little chocolates left on our pillows. Only TINY gripe was the lack of tea/coffee making facilities in the room. Having said that, you're in Venice where there are more cafes than you could shake a stick at. There's only so much caffeine one can drink! I presume that the rooms over looking the very tiny side streets are just as beautiful - it depends whether or not a room with a view is important to you. If you didn't have a great view, no matter as there's a lovely little terrace downstairs from which to sip a coffee or a glass of prosecco and watch the world go by. Breakfast was a basic continental spread (cereals, yoghurt, juice, pastries, cheese, ham, eggs, bread rolls and tea/coffee) but there was plenty of it and it was fine for setting you up for a big day of sightseeing. We were recommended a fantastic restaurant around the corner (Osteria Veccio Pozzo) which apart from the incredible fish does the BEST steak ever (surprising for a small island!). Gianni also booked for us to see a wonderful concert in a palazzo 'La Traviata - Verdi' where we moved to a different room for each of the 3 acts. Alessandro (the manager) and Elena were both really helpful and couldn't do enough to make our stay more welcome. The rest of the staff were the same (sorry, don't know names!) This really was what made this place so special. We've stayed in some amazing hotels in our time and most would need to take lessons from Alessandro and the rest of the staff! We felt welcomed and comfortable and as if nothing was too much trouble. Our parents LOVED Venice and it was made that bit more special by having such a fabulous hotel from which to be based. We never return to the same hotel as we love to visit new places but we have made an exception in this case. We're very much looking forward to staying in the new suites (which are part of the hotel) and are currently under construction - ready in April 2007 I think. Thank you Hotel Antiche Figure, can't wait til next time!

<Author>Jeannella
<Content>Going to Venice? Stay here! Summary: Fantastic value, very highly recommended.My sister and I accompanied my mother on her first trip to Venice, to celebrate her 80th birthday. Mum is fit but has two artificial hips and finds steps difficult. From every point of view the Antiche Figure was the perfect choice of hotel for her and us. The hotel is a five minute walk from the Piazzale Roma where the airport buses terminate, and even less from the railway station. It is very easy to find, as it looks over the canal opposite the station. It is almost at one end of the Grand Canal, so you can hop on a vaporetto and travel the length of the canal in one journey. At the same time it is not so far on foot to Rialto, with its shops and restaurants.The hotel itself is run to the highest standards. It is clean, comfortable, tastefully and appropriately decorated. We had a triple room, and whilst not large, it was adequate. The bathroom was beautiful (though I would agree with a previous reviewer that a shower screen would be an improvement). The linen was spotless, snowy and luxurious and was changed daily. The staff were all helpful and friendly and ready to help with restaurant suggestions, and other enquiries. The breakfast was varied and plentiful. The amenities it offers may warrant a 3 star grading, but their quality is well in excess of that. At the price we paid, it was amazing value.It is hard to fault the hotel. As an Englishwoman, my mother would have liked to find tea-making equipment in the room on arrival - but when in Venice....

<Author>SusanRicketts
<Content>Excellent choice, excellent location Neither of us ever having visited Venice before, I was anxious that my husband's birthday treat should be memorable for all the right reasons! We are both regular users of all the best hotels in the world and although this time we were on a budget, we were highly impressed by the standards that the Antiche Figure offered. Don't be put off that it is only a 3 star listing! The room was spacious, clean and beautifully decorated. We paid the extra for a deluxe canal view room, which are bigger, but on the whole this was an unnecessary extravagance. (In fact, I would imagine that in the high season, it would be a disadvantage, as you are right on the street and the edge of the Grand Canal) I am fanatical about the bed, linen and bathrooms in hotels, but this was all once again well above 3star expectations. The bed was most comfortable and the linen was of superb quality and changed each day. My only reservation about the bathroom, that the shower was screened by a shower curtain (which always have an unpleasant aroma associated with them!) - Why not have a glass screen, this would have been much more fitting with the marble and the murano chandeliers! The hotel was only a 5 minute walk from the bus terminal in Piazzale Roma and surprisingly easy to find. The staff and management were extremely polite and helpful. I would definitely recommend the Antiche Figure to anybocy.Susan Ricketts

<Author>SFHBerks
<Content>Pleasant and Clean Hotel I have to agree with all the other reviews about the location of this hotel. Less than 5 minutes walk from both the railway and bus stations and waterbuses just across the bridge.I spent the weekend there with my 13 year old son and we had a first floor room overlooking the canal. The views were terrific and being just above street level gave us a great feel of being in the thick of it. However the Water buses run through the night so if you need complete silence to sleep perhaps a room higher up or not over looking the canal would be better. But you can't have your cake and eat it and for our part the hustle and bustle was part of the overall great experience.The room was clean tidy and well equipped for a 3* Hotel - my son thought the chocolate each night on the pillow was really cool. As has been said many times the staff were friendly and helpful, even to the extent of phoning the transport department to find out what the orange travel card could be used for.We both thought the breakfast was just right, typical continental and plenty of it. The waitress was diligent in making sure everything was topped up and I thought the orange juice was fine (so full marks to the hotel for taking note of previous reviews).I would wholeheartedly recommend the hotel and should I be lucky enough to visit Venice again I wouldn't hesitate to stay again.Stuart (UK)

I was a little nervous about trying to find a hotel in Venice with our luggage after a long flight. It was so easy to find, we went straight there from the airport shuttle drop off. The bathroom was nice, with a very large tub and a window that opened. This hotel is a good walking distance from St. Marks, but the walk was one of our favorite parts. There were lots of cute shops, markets and restaurants on the way to all the major sights. I would stay here again if returning to Venice. Don't waste your time looking at other hotels. This hotel has it all; great location, service and price!!

<Author>RobDam
<Content>Wonderful stay at Antiche Figure My wife and I stayed at the Antiche Figure for 3 nights at the beginning of December. It was our first time in Venice and we were celebrating our wedding anniversary. We chose the hotel based on the recommendations of this site and we were very happy with our selection. The staff are very helpful in all respects and went out of their way to ensure that we enjoyed our stay They made good recommendations for dinner and gave helpful travel and sightseeing advice. We had Room 211 which was a large room with a small balcony and a lovely view over the Grand Canal. It had a really nice bathroom, with marble floors, his and hers basins and even a bidet. It was also useful having a minibar fridge in the room to store small food items. Our room had a safe for any valuables.The location of the hotel is superb if you are travelling into Venice by bus. It is literally a 5 minute walk from the main bus terminal at Piazalle Roma. With its location directly opposite the Rail terminal (Ferrovia), it is easy to find after your days sightseeing. The vaporetto (water bus) is less than 5 minutes walk from the hotel and will take you to Rialto and St Marco in less than 20 and 40 minutes respectively. Its really easy to walk around Venice as it is very flat, so we appreciated Francesca's advice to only buy a vaporetto ticket for one day for 12 Euros. I thought that the breakfast was great, with cereals, fruits, cold meats, yoghurts, hard boiled eggs, biscuits and plenty more! The lady serving breakfast is very sweet (sorry I don't know her name) and helpful. It was good having access to the internet in the lobby. I would not hesitate to book this hotel again when I return to Venice. For those of you who are still thinking about whether to stay here, don't waste any more time looking elsewhere -just book here - you won't regret it.

<Author>josh_and_robin
<Content>The Grand Canal with a view This is a small hotel with character and friendly staff. The location is convenient and centralized. It sits right on the bank of the Grand Canal across from the train station. The walk to the hotel from the train station is about 150 yards over a bride of stairs (that lack a ramp or handicap access). Neither my wife nor I are handicapped, but I sure felt immobile after dragging 5 luggage bags up and over the stairs. In Venice, you apparently have to have a license to transport luggage or goods over a certain distance. Our options were to take the water Taxi across the 10 yards (I could literately throw a rock at the hotel) of water to the other side for 35 Euros or drag the luggage over the bridge. As you can tell I am still happy about it.The hotel has a small bar and breakfast area on the first floor with a public computer. Our room was on the second floor over looking the Canal. The view is great, but I would recommend a room at the back of the hotel because of the noise from the boats. The room was clean and adequate. It had a tub/shower and large sink. The lighting is poor for women, but it was clean and covered is nice grey marble. The bed was firm, but comfortable. The hotel has free DSL internet and local TV. If you like to watch movies bring your laptop because CNN World news was the only station in English. Overall I would recommend the hotel. Be clear about non-smoking requirements though.FYI: Take a taxi to Murano and donéˆ¥æª› get strong armed into buying from a factory on the spot. Shop around for glass that you like. Once you look in enough stores and factories you will realize that there is a lot of the same stuff for varying prices. If you buy anything over 400 Euros make sure itéˆ¥æªš real Murano glass certified by Vetro Artistico.

<Author>Weisenwolf
<Content>Relaxing Atmosphere, clean tidy and helpful A very tidy Boutique type hotel well maintained and decorated without wrecking the character of an old building. The rooms are clean and tidy and the view if you are at the front is of the Grand Canal is excellent to wake up to. (Well worth a few mores pennies/cents) .The hotel is opposite the train station (not a bad thing; it is not an 'industrial' view) and 5 minutes from it and the bus station and a two minute stroll from a Vaporeto stop. Staff are very friendly and helpful and will happily advise you where it is good to visit and perhaps more importantly what is not. I can't offer much more feedback as we were generally out all day and although breakfast was included for us we only made breakfast on one occasion as we prefer to grab something while out and about but it appeared decent as these continental buffet arrangements go (I still prefer a Venetian snack from a Street vendor myself. Make sure you get yourselves a Vapporeto (boat bus) ticket to cover the period you are there (They do 24/36/48 hour tickets etc. you can get them from the stop over the bridge next to the train station) and you can just jump on and jump off when you feel like it. They are like London buses arriving every few minutes and there are few places more than a 5 minute stroll or a 15 minute saunter from a Vapo stop.Get a good guide book (Eyewitness with the 3D maps are particularly good for the Grand Canal) and follow the advice on eateries in Venice as they are a bit variable in quality. If you like seafood head for the fish market and if you stand on the stone bridge running alongside the grand canal and look inland there is a little wooden bridge which leads to an excellent seafood restaurant (I think it is called the Antiche something or the other) for a quiet high quality meal that will not break the bank. Turbot for two I would heartily recommend with a lobster gnocchi starter or the seafood soup. Good wine list too.

<Author>brianshodge
<Content>A Wonderful End to a Dream Vacation! The hotel is in a beautiful historical building near the beginning of the Grand Canal. It is just a 5 minute walk from Piazzale Roma (where you first begin your journey into Venice if going by car). Remember that if you have a lot of luggage you will have to pass over two bridges with stairs to get to the hotel so pack light or bring strong arms. When compared to any other hotel in Venice, however, two bridges to cross is nothing! The hotel is within a 30 minute walk to San Marco Square and there is a really nice area with shops just around the corner from the hotel as well. The accomodations were spotless and spacious and I didn't have a Canal view room. The bathroom was beautifully done in marble and murano glass. Most importantly, service was 5 star and exceeds any Hilton, Marriott or other hotel with more stars that I have ever stayed in. 3 Star Superior? This hotel's staff sets it at a standard above the rest and deserves a 4 Star Superior in my view.

<Author>ejs
<Content>Solid hotel for quick visit This is a solid but not spectacular hotel. The best thing about this hotel is the location. When people say it is across from the train station next to the green dome, they mean directly across the grand canal from the train station. I forgot my watch and looked out the window at the train station clock for the time. When leaving by train, just walk across the bridge, no hassle worrying about being late for the train. If getting in by bus it is a block or two walk so if your luggage has wheels, no problem. I went to the right instead of straight and to the left where the bus dropped us off and went to the side canal which is pretty big and thought it was the grand canal. Just asked where the train station was and got pointed in the right direction. If staying for a long time, there are better hotels in quieter areas on side canals. There are no real balconies where you can hang out and watch the grand canal and the windows are just a little too high to get a good view. Breakfast is plain, don't think of it as a big meal.. just enough to get you to lunch. The staff is very nice. They will only recommend two restaurants and the one in back which is accessed on the alley is cheaper and I thought it was better than the more expensive one by the first bridge which is a step up in class but harder to find. They were just puttin up their website and it wasn't in English yet but should be ready by now. If you book directly with them they will give you a better deal if you upgrade your room. The room they booked for us was too small and we upgraded to a bigger room with a canal view. If anyone makes a suggestion they try and implement it. Someone wanted internet access so they put a laptop by the front desk you can use free of charge to access your email. There are better hotels, but if you only have a few days, the location and clealiness make this a solid choice. It takes you a day to figure out the vaporeto schedule, but they start the line a block away by the bus stop so walk down there and you always get a good seat, often in the front or back rather than inside. Avoid the #1, take the #86 whenever possible and don't worry, almost every one stops at the train station to get back if you don't want to walk. As you are at the far end of town, it makes you get out and travel. We walked from here to St. Marks but only one way and takes awile. Get off at the Rialto bridge which is the most crowded stop and walk to St. Marks. Safe at night so we went there every day and night and usually got back midnight to 1am and the desk clerk didn't mind. Posting an arrow above streets telling you how to get to major areas is a big plus, I wish they did that in Rome. You never feel you are lost and always felt safe even walking around after midnight.  
<Date>Nov 15, 2006

<Content>Karen and John Adamthwaite, Newcastle, NSW Australia - Loved it Antiche Figure, Venice, Italy.Date 26/27October 2006.What a great hotel. We had a booking for four couples, two had booked canal view rooms and the other two normal rooms. We had just arrived off the Marco Polo Cruise and had to walk from the overseas terminal to the hotel as no transport was available so we just followed the signs to Piazzale Roma and then followed the signs to the trains station. Only took 15 minutes in total. Ten of us arrived at the hotel at 9.30am, eight were staying and the other couple we travelling from Venice to Rome by train at 1pm. On our arrival Alessandro was marvellous he allowed our other friends to leave their luggage until they left on the train and that allowed them to explore Venice for a few hours.From the moment we walked in Alessandro was only too pleased to assist us with maps and information on Venice. We stayed two nights (not enough) and that afternoon we bought a 24 hour Vaporetta ticket from across the Canal, good value. Only takes 10 minutes to get to St Mark's Square and it is an exciting way to travel around Venice, especially when you do not have much time. We also used the ticket to go over to the island of Lido, what a pretty place, it even has cars and buses.Before our arrival at the Antiche Figure I emailed them and asked if they could book the Secret Itinerary of Doge's Palace which they did so without any bother. Francesca emailed me a booking number and all we had to do was arrive there and go to the Information desk and get out tickets. This tour takes you to parts of Doge's Palace that the general tours do not take you. Well worth it. Two of us had canal view rooms, and the other two couples had the other rooms. All four rooms we great. My room was 411 and every morning I would stand at the window and look at all the traffic and goings on on the grand canal, loved it. Bathroom was huge and our bedroom was huge. It is lovely to sit out at the tables out the front of the hotel and have a few glasses of wine and just people watch.This hotel has everything, even free internet access in the lobby. How good is that., especially when internet cafes charge so much throughout Italy.This was the best hotel we stayed at during our 4 weeks away and would have no hesitation in staying there again, even if I couldn't get a canal view room. All four couples found this to be the best, not one complaint.Congragulations Alessandro, Francesca, and the lovely lady who served us our wine of an afternoon, I'm sorry I didn't get your name. <Author>Boulevardier
<Content>Spirit of Venice This hotel is excellently situated, close to the railway station all the important vaporetti stops are just over the canal. The rooms are superb, elegantly and well appointed, the staff friendly, efficient and fun. The georgeous Francesca managed my late request for the laundering of my shirts with great alacrity. It is a great place for people watching, a Birra Moretti, or Campari Soda taken on the tables outside in the evening provide an insight into the protocol of the gondoliers who operate from their well-appointed cabin on the quay. They always seem pre-booked when asked by middle-aged couples, but are, nor surprisngly, available when requested by skimpily-clad antipodean girls! C'est la vie - or the Venetian equivalent! Although a busy frontage, there is no street crime and the ambience is is one of studied insoucience.Good restaurants close by - the Ostaria Vecio Pozzo just around the corner in Corte Canal is excellent - the mussels are a treat and thr range of wines interesting.

<Author>citeseer
<Content>All we'd hoped for We chose this hotel based on Tripadvisor reviews - and are glad we did. It was all we'd hoped for. We arrived by train and it's very reassuring to see the hotel as soon as you emerge from the Station. Venice is a maze and full of people dragging luggage over cobblestones and up and down steps, we were glad this wasn't us! The location of Antiche Figure is excellent. It's just far enough from the Station (on the other side of the Grand Canal) not to be a Station Hotel but is within easy walking or vaporetto distance to all the sights. After our forays to Piazza San Marco and the Rialto, we were glad that our hotel wasn't there! All of Venice is crowded with tourists but some parts are even worse than others. Our room was quite small, Alessandro said we could change if we wanted to but we chose to stay as, although we hadn't paid for a canal view, this room did, in fact, have a good view of the canal from the side windows. Reception were very helpful and made us feel most welcome. On arrival, hours before check-in, Alessandro took in our luggage, gave us a map and pointed out our Venice familiarisation tour via vaporetto! On his suggestion we bought a 3-day vaporetto pass which turned out ot be an excellent investment. Later he made bookings for us on the Secret Itinerary Tour at the Palazzo Ducale so we didn't have to queue. My husband and I would happily recommend Antiche Figure as THE place to stay on a trip to Venice.

<Author>swy94611
<Content>Can't go wrong with Hotel Antiche Figure Everything was great about the hotel! The location was perfect for us as we were there for a pre-cruise stay. Everything is within walking distance and it's so easy to catch the water buses. Regarding the noise - If you don't leave any of the windows open, you don't hear any of the canal or street noise as all the windows are double paned. (Also the mosquitoes don't come in!!) The canal rooms are worth the upgrade as they are slightly larger than the interior rooms. Breakfast was good. There were fresh fruits, yogurt, cheese, cold cuts and bread/pastries. Can't comment on the coffee as I didn't have any. There were at least two juice selections. Hard-boiled eggs were available, but I don't recall if they served scrambled eggs or not. The selection of food is much better than some of the other hotels I stayed at in Europe from previous trips. The staff made sure that there was enough food selection for everyone.Alessandro and Francesca were extremely helpful. They answered all my e-mails promptly and even helped in getting some tickets for us. The only thing that I didn't quite understand was that when we booked 11 rooms nine months ago, 4 were for canal view rooms. When we arrived, we were informed that they had overbooked the canal view rooms the following day and wanted to know if anyone in our party was interested in moving to an interior room. One member in our party volunteered to move and in fact, he liked his second room better than the canal view room he had on the first floor! Again, this hotel is great. You will enjoy your stay there.

<Author>HLinkowich
<Content>Beautiful Hotel But SO Noisy! We stayed at this hotel for two nights. Upon arrival, we were given a Canal View room which is what we paid for on the first floor. I was concerned about the noise level since there seemed to be a lot of activity outside, but I was assured that there are no cars in Venice so it would be quiet. During the day, the view from our room was great and the location was fantastic. The people were friendly and helpful and the room was spacious. They definitely have a mold problem at least in our bathroom in room 112 in which they may want to invest in a Bleach pen. We fight mold at our house, too, but this did not seem to be in control. We returned to our room at 9:30 pm to settle in for the evening and between the foot traffic and boats on the canal, it seemed to be noisier than a freeway. In addition, people stopped at the hotel tables outside to have a drink on the canal and were not very respectful to those of us who were exhausted from a long day of sightseeing. It finally calms down after 11 pm and starts right back up at 4 am when I heard the rolling of suitcases heading toward the bus stop and the vaporetti begins again. We would have changed rooms the next evening but our flight was at 6 am from Venice airport so we knew we wouldn't need to sleep later than 4 am, so we just stuck it out. If you are a heavy sleeper and can sleep through anything, this hotel is wonderful. However, if you are a light (me) to moderate (my husband) sleeper, do not get a canal view room. You will not sleep or even rest due to the noise level.

<Author>Diggerr
<Content>Lovely stay and highly recommended This was our first visit to Venice and we stayed at the Hotel Antiche Figure. If you are in the same situation as we were and wondering where to stay, stop dithering and book here - you will not regret it. Although we travelled to Venice on the ferry from Croatia (highly recommended!), we caught the train to Treviso and flew back to the UK from Treviso airport; however, for people arriving in Venice by train, being directly opposite the Railway Station makes the hotel very accessible and easy to find. When researching where to stay in Venice a recurring theme was the difficulties people had finding their hotels (particularly in the dark) and also carrying their luggage around Venice. You will not have those problems here.

<Author>TLIII
<Content>Great little hotel, with a lot of charm My family and I (6 people in total) stayed at the Antiche Figure on the night of August 30th (following our 12 night Mediterranean cruise). We chose this classy small hotel based on the glowing reviews we'd read on trip advisor.The hotel lived up to our expectations because it truly is a charming little hotel (more like a BB), dramatically located on the Grand Canal - offering breathtaking views of the Grand Canal.Our family had two rooms (#412 and #211). The tv's carried CNN News and BBC (really the only two English speaking channels available to us).The best thing about the hotel - other than its favorable canal front setting - is their personable front office staff. Elena, Franchesca and Alessandro were top notch! They were friendly, informative and helpful. Franchesca recommended a nice little restaurant to us which was located only a couple of minute stroll from the hotel (the Ostaria al Vecio Pozzo). Its nothing fancy, as its located in a small alley way, however, the food was very good and reasonably priced.One of the things we learned while dining at restaurants around the Mediterranean during our cruise is that you should expect to pay a cover charge to eat in the restaurant. Most of the cover charges ranged from 2 to 3 euros per person (that's right, it typically costed us $2.50 to $3.50 per person just to sit down in the restaurant - a ridiculous fee, but one that seemed to be standard wherever we ate). Plus, you could expect to pay a service charge of 10 to 13 percent (which we were consistently told was to pay for the restaurant ambiance and the rolls they brought us when we sat down). THEN, you are expected to leave a tip for the waitstaff! Europeans should never complain about eating in U.S. restaurants because they won't be hit with these same types of fees!The Antiche Figure has a small breakfast room where a complimentary continental breakfast is served (traditional european style continental breakfast with hams, cheeses, cereals, croissants, rolls, juices, coffee, teas, etc). Nice, but nothing fancy.Elena was very helpful in arranging a water taxi for us to go to the airport in the morning. Let me point out a few things which will be helpful to you in terms of the best ways to get around Venice from this hotel...As you know, probably the best way to explore Venice is by foot! The hotel is a 15 minute leisurely walk from the Rialto Bridge (a very overrated sightseeing attraction!). The Rialto Bridge is a 15 minute walk from San Marco Square (the major tourist attraction in Venice which was always mobbed with tourists). We had fun feeding the pigeons there and shopping in the seemingly endless glass boutiques! As previous reviews have mentioned, it is VERY EASY to find your way back through the maze of small side streets, because you simply follow the signs for Ferrazzi (not sure on the spelling of it) - which means train station. The train station is located directly across the canal from the hotel, however, you really don't hear any noise from there other than the occasional street singers/musicians who perform at the base of the steps.Franchesca advised us to take Water Taxi #1 (located only a two minute walk from the front of the hotel) in order to have a nice cruise down the Grand Canal. The water taxi ride was 5 euros per person and enabled us to go down the entire Grand Canal (we got off at San Marco Square and walked back). She also recommended that we use the services of the gondoliers located outside the front entrance of the hotel, since we wanted to experience one of Venice's famous gondola rides. The 40 minute gondola ride we opted to take cost us 100 euros (which seemed on par with what two other gondoliers near San Marco Plaza had quoted me). The gondola ride was very fun and definitely worth taking in order to experience Venice's small canals! Plus, if you take the gondola ride from the guys located in front of the hotel, you know you'll get your money's worth!The most economical way to get to Marco Polo Airport is via bus (the bus fare is only 3 euros per person from the bus terminal to the airport). The bus depot is only a five minute walk from the hotel - however, if you are dragging/carrying luggage, be advised that you have to cross two small bridges. Our family opted for the much pricier private water taxi ride (which cost us 120 euros in total) only because of the convenience of it. The water taxi picked us up right outside the hotel entrance and only took 25 minutes to get to the airport! We had lots of luggage, so it made sense to take the water taxi (despite the much higher cost). Allesandro was very helpful getting us settled into the water taxi in the morning. If you are travelling alone or with one or two other people, I would strongly advise just taking the bus. Also, please be aware that once you get to the airport via water taxi, you still have to walk about four minutes from the dock area to the airport terminal. It's a very ease walk though. When our water taxi pulled in, we were asked if we wanted help taking our luggage over to the airport. Be aware that the porters/luggage handlers were looking to charge us 4 1/2 euros per bag for this service. We quickly decided to haul our own luggage instead (the airport has small luggage carts that you can use at no extra charge).We enjoyed our stay in Venice very much. It's such a quaint little city and truly unique with its endless canal system. Like nothing you'll ever see anywhere else in the world! We all said that we'd definitely return to stay at the Antiche Figure hotel when we return to Venice. If you are looking for a hotel with more amenities (like fitness equipment, a dinner restaurant, etc), you are probably better off staying at a bigger property. However, the Antiche Figure is a great value because of its high level of personal service and great canal location (even if it is a 30 minute walk from the main tourist area of San Marco).
